# 6.1 User Procedures

## 6.1.1 User and SRB1 setup in gNB-DU - Initial Access (3GPP SA)

### 6.1.1.0-2 User and SRB1 setup in gNB-DU - Initial Access (3GPP SA) 13339576: User and SRB1 setup in gNB-DU - Initial Access (3GPP SA) 13339576: User and SRB1 setup in gNB-DU - Initial Access (3GPP SA) 13339576: User and SRB1 setup in gNB-DU - Initial Access (3GPP SA) 13339576: User and SRB1 setup in gNB-DU - Initial Access (3GPP SA) 13339576: User and SRB1 setup in gNB-DU - Initial Access (3GPP SA) 13339576: User and SRB1 setup in gNB-DU - Initial Access (3GPP SA) 13339576: User and SRB1 setup in gNB-DU - Initial Access (3GPP SA) 13339576: User and SRB1 setup in gNB-DU - Initial Access (3GPP SA) 13339576: User and SRB1 setup in gNB-DU - Initial Access (3GPP SA) [image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "User and SRB1 setup in gNB-DU-Initial Access (3GPP SA)". The diagram depicts interactions between different components: 5G-L2-PS, 5G-L2-LO, 5G-L2-HIDU, and 5G C-Plane. The diagram begins with a "par" block, indicating parallel execution. 1. 5G C-Plane initiates a request to 5G-L2-HIDU with PsUser_UserSetupReq(User Setup + SRB1) . 2. 5G-L2-HIDU then sends a request to 5G-L2-LO with LoUser_UserSetupReq(UserSetup+SRB1) . 3. Simultaneously, 5G-L2-HIDU also initiates a timer rdL2LoTempUeTimer and rdL2PsTempUeTimer with the following details: * Start: Initial Access * Expiry: Temporary UE context deletion any time before successful User Setup requested by C-Plane. 4. 5G-L2-LO receives the request and displays a message: "User setup (temporary user changed to pemmanent one). Bearer setup(SRB1)." 5. 5G-L2-LO then sends a response to 5G-L2-HIDU with LoUser_UserSetupResp . 6. 5G-L2-HIDU receives the response and displays a message: "User setup (temporary user changed to pemmanent one). Bearer setup(SRB1)." 7. 5G-L2-HIDU also initiates a timer rdL2PsTempUeTimer (stop temporary UE context supervision) . 8. 5G-L2-HIDU sends a request to 5G-L2-PS with PsUser_UserSetupResp . 9. 5G-L2-PS receives the response. 10. 5G-L2-HIDU sends a request to 5G C-Plane with HUserDu_BearerSetuoReq (SRE1) . 11. A message "SRB1 Setup" is displayed. 12. 5G C-Plane sends a response to 5G-L2-HIDU with HUserDu_Bearer Setuo Resp (SRE1) . The bottom right corner contains the URL: http://msc-generator.sourceforge.net v8.3.7 .[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/5G_L1L2_FLOW_124_User+SRB1setup DU(Initial Access).png[/image_path][/image-0] 5G_L1L2_FLOW_124_User+SRB1setup DU(Initial Access).signalling (ID: 13339576)

The diagram depicts interactions between several components: TargetCell, SourceCell, and 5G C-Plane. Within the SourceCell, there are sub-components: 5G-L2-PS, 5G-L2-LO, and 5G-L2-HIDU. The sequence of events begins with a PsUser_UserSetupReq message from SourceCell (5G-L2-PS) to TargetCell (5G-L2-PS), carrying UserSetup , SRB1 , SRB2 , and DRB information. This is followed by a PsUser_UserSetupResp from TargetCell to SourceCell, returning a CRNTI . Next, a LoUser_UserSetupReq is sent from SourceCell (5G-L2-LO) to TargetCell (5G-L2-LO), including UserSetup , SRB1 , SRB2 , DRB , and CRNTI . TargetCell responds with LoUser_UserSetupResp . A key step involves PsUser_UserSuspendSchedulingReq from SourceCell (5G-L2-PS) to TargetCell (5G-L2-PS), with a note indicating that "5G-L2-PS suspends DL and UL DRB scheduling in the source cell." This is acknowledged by PsUser_UserSuspendSchedulingResp . The diagram then shows a parallel process ( par ) initiated by SourceCell (5G-L2-HIDU) to TargetCell (5G-L2-HIDU) for SRB1 setup, involving HiUserDu_BearerModifyReq(SRB1) and HiUserDu_BearerModifyResp(SRB1) . Similarly, for SRB2 setup, HiUserDu_BearerModifyReq(SRB2) is sent from SourceCell (5G-L2-HIDU) to TargetCell (5G-L2-HIDU), followed by HiUserDu_BearerModifyResp(SRB2) . A loop ( loop ) is depicted for DRB setup, where HiUserDu_BearerModifyReq(DRB) is sent from SourceCell (5G-L2-HIDU) to TargetCell (5G-L2-HIDU), followed by HiUserDu_BearerModifyResp(DRB) . A note clarifies that "In case of multiple DRBs to be setup, HiUserDU_BearerModifyReq shall be sent for each DRB to be modified." There are also two text boxes providing context: 1. "In Intra DU HO case, the user context setup for the target cell shall have a different ueldDu regarding the old context of the source cell and a different nrcellidentity along with different CRNTI with which the old and newuser context is differentiated." 2. "In Intra DU HO case, the user context setup for the target cell shall have a different nrcellidentity along with different CRNTI with wich the old and new user context is differentiated." Another text box explains: "HiUserDu_BearerModifyReq is sent after the PsUser_UserSuspendSchedulingReq to ensure that there is no UL data received from the old L2-PS user context to L2-HI DU which is now configured with the new TEID." Finally, a URL is present at the bottom right: https://gitlab.com/msc-generator v8.2 .[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m1dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_Flows_file_403.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] Note: If the UE is CA configured where two L2-PS instances are involved, the parameter ueSuspendCause in the messages PsUserSuspendSchedulingReq send to each L2-PS instances (supporting respectively the PCell and the SCell)  has to be set to the value unknown (ID: 11180060)

**6.1.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11180070`)

User Setup in gNB-DU - Intra DU Handover (3GPP SA)
MSC 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_218: SCELL SUSPEND (Intra-GNB Intra-DU Handover for Inter-L2RT CA UE)

Refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_218

Note: the parameter ueSuspendCause in the message PsUserSuspendSchedulingReq has to be set to the value Unknown

---

**6.1.2.0-3**  (ID: `11180079`)

User Setup in gNB-DU - Intra DU Handover (3GPP SA)
UserSetup Procedure for URLLC

In case of low latency demo, L2-RT has the core deployment as specified in 5G\_RAN\_UP\_15925. All EO's and EQ's mentioned below are URLLC-specific.

Upon reception of PsUser\_UserSetupReq  message, L2-PS triggers User Setup procedure. PsUser in Sgnl EO of this component forwards received indication to both UL EO and DL EO.

Upon reception of LoUser\_UserSetupReq message, L2-LO triggers User Setup procedure. DL EO of this component forwards received indication to UL EO.

---

Here's a breakdown of the interactions: 1. 5G-L2-PS to 5G C-Plane: * An optional message [5GC000478-A] PsCell_CellSetupReq(...,actGnblnitRlf,...) is sent. * The 5G-L2-PS component configures and activates "Radio Link Failure detection &amp; indication in 5G-L2-PS instance". * A response PsCell_CellSetupResp is received. * A message "UE context is created" is indicated. 2. 5G-L1-UL to 5G-L2-PS: * "PUCCH scheduling" is performed. * Several UIData_PucchReceiveReq , UIData_PucchReceiveRespPsU , UIData_PucchReceiveRespPsD , and UIData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD messages are exchanged. 3. 5G-L2-PS to 5G C-Plane (Radio Link Status Indications): * Scenario 1: RLF Detected * An optional message "Radio Link Status: 'RLF detected'" is sent. * A message [5GC000478-A] PsUser_RadioLinkStatusInd(ueRIStatus=[rlf_dl_harqOR rlf_bsi_csi]) is sent to the 5G C-Plane. * The 5G C-Plane receives a message [5GC000478-D] Cause value: 'rlf_bsi_csi'is supported. * Scenario 2: RLF Not Detected * An optional message "Radio Link Status: 'RLF not detected'" is sent. * A message [5GC000478-A] PsUser_RadioLinkStatusInd(ueRIStatus=rf_off) is sent to the 5G C-Plane. ## 6.1.4 User reconfiguration required indication

### 6.1.4.1 Call flow

#### 6.1.4.1.0-2 Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow 13251234: Call flow [image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "User reconfiguration required indication" process in a 5G network. The diagram depicts interactions between two entities: "5G-L2-PS" and "5G C-Plane," along with a "Timer." The sequence of events is as follows: 1. (10) UE Context is created: This is the initial state, indicating that a User Equipment (UE) context has been established. 2. (20) Need for User reconfiguration detected: The 5G-L2-PS detects a need for user reconfiguration. 3. (30) PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd: The 5G-L2-PS sends a "PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd" message to the 5G C-Plane. Following this, there are two alternative paths (Alt) based on whether a "PsUser_UserModifyReq" message is received before the timer expires. Alternative 1: No PsUser_UserModifyReq received before Timer Expiry * (60) No PsUser_UserModifyReq recieved before Timer Expiry: This condition signifies that the 5G-L2-PS does not receive the "PsUser_UserModifyReq" message within the expected timeframe. * (80) PsUser_UserModifyReq: This message is shown as not being sent in this branch. * (90) waitTimer start: The timer starts. * (160) Timer expiry: The timer expires. * (180) The procedure shall be considered as failed: As a consequence of the timer expiring without receiving the expected message, the procedure is marked as failed. Alternative 2: PsUser_UserModifyReq received This alternative is further divided into two sub-alternatives: "Successful RRC reconf" and "Unsuccessful RRC reconf." * Successful RRC reconf: * (100) Successful RRC reconf: This condition indicates a successful Radio Resource Control (RRC) reconfiguration. * (110) PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq: The 5G-L2-PS sends a "PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq" message to the 5G C-Plane. * (120) waitTimer stop: The timer is stopped. * Unsuccessful RRC reconf: * (130) Unsuccessful RRC reconf: This condition indicates an unsuccessful RRC reconfiguration. * (140) PsUser_UserModifyReq: The 5G-L2-PS sends a "PsUser_UserModifyReq" message to the 5G C-Plane. * (150) waitTimer stop: The timer is stopped. Finally, there is a separate event related to the timer: * (170) waitTimer Expiry: This event is shown as a dashed line, suggesting it's a potential outcome or a related timer event, possibly linked to the unsuccessful reconfiguration path or a general timer expiry. The diagram uses standard UML sequence diagram notation, with lifelines representing the entities and arrows indicating messages exchanged between them. The dashed lines represent timer events.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-11201651.png[/image_path][/image-0] 5G_L1L2_FLOW_133_User_reconfiguration_required_indication-CNI-136896.signalling (ID: 13251234)

### 6.1.4.2 Description

#### 6.1.4.2.0-1 Description (20) Note (ID: 11180140)

**6.1.4.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11180147`)

Description
L2-PS detects need for User reconfiguration: Number of SRS Ports reconfiguration or any other.

---

#### 6.1.4.2.0-2 Description (30) Message PsUser_ReconfigurationrequiredInd (ID: 11180154)

**6.1.4.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11180161`)

Description
The message indicated the cause for reconfiguration to 5G C-Plane.

---

**6.1.4.2.0-3**  (ID: `11180169`)

Description
[Before CNI-136896]

**(50)** Message PsUser\_UserModifyReq\*\*\*\*

**[End CNI-136896]**

---

**6.1.4.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11180176`)

Description
[Before CNI-136896]

Parameters indicate to L2-PS the reconfiguration is **denied by 5G C-Plane.**

[End CNI-136896]

---

#### 6.1.4.2.0-4 Description (80) Message PsUser_UserModifyReq (ID: 11180183)

**6.1.4.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11180190`)

Description
Parameters indicate to L2-PS the reconfiguration is accepted by 5G C-Plane.

---

#### 6.1.4.2.0-5 Description (100) Alternative: Successful RRC reconf (ID: 11180199)

**6.1.4.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11180205`)

Description
Upon successfull completion of RRC reconfiguration, C-Plane shall acknowledge the reconfiguration.

---

#### 6.1.4.2.0-6 Description (130) Alternative: Unsuccessful RRC reconf (ID: 11180212)

**6.1.4.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11180219`)

Description
Upon unsuccessfull completion of RRC reconfiguration, C-Plane shall inform the U-Plane of the reconfiguration failure.

---

#### 6.1.4.2.0-7 Description (140) Message PsUser_UserModifyReq (ID: 11180226)

**6.1.4.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11180233`)

Description
Parameters indicate to L2-PS the reconfiguration is cancelled.

---

#### 6.1.4.2.0-8 Description (180) Note (ID: 11180239)

**6.1.4.2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11180245`)

Description
In case neither PsUSer\_RrcReconfCompletedReq nor cancellation is received in L2-PS from C-Plane, the procedure shall be considered as failed.

---

(10) UE Context is created : This is an initial event, likely a setup phase. 2. (20) Need for User reconfiguration detected : The 5G-L2-PS detects a need for user reconfiguration. 3. (30) PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredind : The 5G-L2-PS sends a "PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredind" message to the 5G C-Plane. UlData_SrsReceiveReq for pSRS is not sent during the SRS traisient phase from step (70) to (110) (ID: 11180306)

### 6.1.4.3-2 Message Flow for "No Additional Dl Dmrs" reconfiguration

#### 6.1.4.3-2.0-2 Message Flow for "No Additional Dl Dmrs" reconfiguration Description (ID: 11180334)

**6.1.4.3-2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11180347`)

Message Flow for "No Additional Dl Dmrs" reconfiguration
Scell: DRX and Pcell's pSRS slot offset is configured from PsUser\_UserModifyReq

1)DRX: apply the fakeDrx or normal DRX configuration from CPRT

2)PUSCH:

- FDD UL: last /two PUSCH symbol is skipped on PCell’s pSRS slot offset, refer to 5G\_L2\_11462\_replaced([11162112](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25eTvfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

- TDD UL: not supported in currrent release

3)PDSCH:

-- FDD DL: last two PDSCH symbol is skipped on Pcell's WBTAS SRS slot offset or 4/9 slot is skipped for Critical band(txSwitchImpactToRx),refer to 5G\_L2\_15411\_replaced([11162192](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25e6wfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

3)PDSCH:

-- FDD DL: last two PDSCH symbol is skipped on Pcell's WBTAS SRS slot offset or 4/9 slot is skipped for Critical band(txSwitchImpactToRx),refer to 5G\_L2\_15411\_replaced([11162192](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25e6wfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

The diagram is structured with a main flow initiated by "opt: when No Addtional DL DMRS switch triggered". This leads to a message "(0)PsUser\_Reconfiguration RequiredInd with "No Aditional DI Dmrs" reconfig requirement" sent from 5G-L2-PS to 5G-CP-RT.
Following this, there are several alternative paths (Alt 1, Alt 2, Alt 3, Alt 4) and optional steps ("opt may delay sometime if DPA interworking").
**Alt 1** describes the scenario where the "No Additional DI Dmrs" change is successful for the UE on air. This involves messages like "(1.1)PsUser\_UserModify Req with "No Additional DL DMRS" modification", "(1.2) PsUser\_UserModify Resp, UE enter transient phase", and "(1.3)PsUser\_RrcReconfCompleted Req, end transient phase, new parameter take effect".
**Alt 2** covers the case where the "No Additional DI Dmrs" change fails. This path includes messages such as "(2.1)PsUser\_UserModify Req with "No Additional DL DMRS" modification" and "(2.3) PsUser\_UserModify Resp, UE enter transient phase". It also shows a message "(2.3)PsUser\_UserModify Req with change cancel, UE ends transient phase, roll back to legacy parameter".
**Alt 3** indicates that "PsUser\_Reconfiguration RequiredInd is ignored by CP but there is parellel reconfiguration from CP". This leads to "(3.1)PsUser\_UserModify Req without "No Additional DL DMRS" change" and a note "(3.2)for No Additional DI Dmrs RRC reconfiguration procedure, end it when timer expire as 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_5636".
**Alt 4** states that "PsUser\_Reconfiguration RequiredInd is ignored by CP". This is followed by a note "(4.1)for No Additional DI Dmrs RRC reconfiguration procedure, end it when timer expire as 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_5636".

## 6.1.6 RRC Connection Re-establishment

### 6.1.6.1 Call flow:

#### 6.1.6.1.0-5 Call flow: 13368594: Call flow: 13368594: Call flow: 13368594: Call flow: 13368594: Call flow: 13368594: Call flow: 13368594: Call flow: 13368594: Call flow: 13368594: Call flow: 13368594: Call flow: 13368594: Call flow: 13368594: Call flow: 13368594: Call flow: [image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the RRC Connection Re-establishment procedure in a 5G network. The diagram depicts interactions between different network functions, including 5G-L2-LO, 5G-L2-PS, 5G-L2-HI DU, 5G-CP, 5G-L2-HI CU, and 5G-L2-SRB. The diagram is structured with vertical lifelines representing each network function and horizontal arrows indicating messages exchanged between them. The messages are numbered and often enclosed in boxes with labels describing the action or data being transmitted. Conditional logic is represented using "Opt" (optional) blocks. Key messages and interactions include: * RRC Reestablishment and Reestablishment Complete: Messages (2) and (3) indicate DL and UL data on SRB in gNB-CU related to RRC Reestablishment and Reestablishment Complete. * SN Status Transfer: Several "Opt" blocks handle scenarios where SN Status Transfer is received before or not expected during Reestablishment Request. These trigger bearer modification requests and responses. * Bearer Modification: Messages like HiUserCu_BearerModifyReq , HiUserCu_BearerModifyResp , HiUserDu_BearerModifyReq , HiUserDu_BearerModifyResp , PsUser_UserModifyReq , PsUser_UserModifyResp , LoUser_UserModifyReq , and LoUser_UserModifyResp are exchanged for modifying bearers, with causes specified such as "FetchResource", "Suspend", "Resume", and "BearerSetup". * Data Transmission: Message (12) and (13) are similar to (2) and (3) but appear later in the diagram. A "DU DL data transmission unblock" message is shown. * First UL Packet: Message (19.1) indicates the reception of the first UL packet. * Data Reception and PDU Transmission: LoData_UlRlcPduReceiveInd (20) and GTP-U PDU (F1-U DDDS) (21) are shown. * Monitoring: PsUser_DIBufferMonitoringInd (23) is the final message shown. The diagram outlines a complex process with multiple optional paths and conditions, reflecting the dynamic nature of RRC connection re-establishment in a 5G environment.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/a9f81d4f-96bf-4ef9-94a7-75fe87229330.png[/image_path][/image-0] [CNI-136896-J] Conv erted to PlantUML [End CNI-136896-J] **** (ID: 13368594)

**6.1.6.2.0-11.0-2**  (ID: `11180673`)

Description:
At the reception of HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq with cause= [Before CB008490-CIF] MobilitySuspend [CB008490-CIF] Suspend [End CB008490-CIF] with securityParams is filled, pdcpCountRequired = FALSE, 5G-L2-HI (CU):

* suspends DL data
* PDCP Reestablishment
* configures F1-U DL TEID
* pdcpCounts are not present
* configures the ciphering algorithm and security key
* for the UL PDCU PDU(s) received over the source F1-U and X2-U tunnel, the previous security key shall be used for deciphering
* for the UL PDCU PDU(s) received over the target F1-U and X2-U tunnel, the security key provided in the HiUserCu\_BearerModify with securityParams is filled shall be used for deciphering

**6.1.6.2.0-26.0-3**  (ID: `11180909`)

Description:
If ((RRC Reestablishment is during Inter-gNB Handover via Xn or NG) and (XnAP: SN Status Transfer or NGAP:Downlink RAN Status Transfer is received after RRC Reestablishment request)).

At the reception of HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq with cause= BearerSetup and securityParams is filled, 5G-L2-HI (CU):

* configures PDCP COUNT
* configures DL TEID in PDCP
* configures security parameters for the UL PDCP PDU(s) (encryption or/and integrity protection)
* starts DL data transsmission

else

At the reception of HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq with cause= [Before CB008490-CIF] MobilityResume [CB008490-CIF] Resume [End CB008490-CIF], 5G-L2-HI (CU):

* resumes data transsmission
* continues  data forwarding if requested
* disable flow control  for 5QI-1, 5QI-2 bearers
* sets discard timer for 5QI-1 if flow control is disabled
* release old UL F1-U TEID

**6.1.7.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11181092`)

Description
In Interfreq HO case, the L2-PS will receive measurement gap configuration from CP-RT to suspend all UL and DL scheduling for the UE who performs the inter-freq measurement accordingly 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4189\_replaced([11174355](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4805\_replaced([11194818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv3fd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

DRX config can be enabled by message PsUser\_UserModifyReq() and PsUser\_UserSetupReq(refer 5G\_L2\_IF\_389\_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

[before 5GC000772-C]the field "numOfDrxConfig" set to 1(it means there is drxconfig in message) and field "drxConfig" of drxConfig structure in PCell config set to 1(it means enable the DRX).

[5GC000772-C]the field "drxConfig" of drxConfig structure set to 1(it means enable the DRX).

If DRX is already enabled, it will ignore the messages.  
The activation procedure is prefer(5G\_UP\_ALG\_2263\_replaced([11114367](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpkDK_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

so DRX enable like bellow:

Link to the "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_3997\_RegularDrxToSpecialDrx.signalling" file:
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the process of configuring regular DRX to special DRX when entering the SAG ON state. The diagram depicts interactions between a "SAG eligible UE with VoNR bearer setup, DRX Profile2 has been enabled" and two network components: "PCell" and "SCell", both identified as "5G-L2-PS".
The sequence of events is as follows:
1. **Initial State**: The UE is eligible for VoNR bearer setup and DRX Profile2 has been enabled.
2. **Reconfiguration Required**: The UE sends a `PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd` message to the network, indicating `TransformPrecoderInd=enabled`.
3. **User Modify Request (UE to Network)**: The UE sends a `PsUser_UserModifyReq` message to the network with `transformPrecoderSwitchAck=TRUE` and `drxConfig=Special DRX Config`.
4. **User Modify Request (UE to SCell)**: A sub-message `PsUser_UserModifyReq` is sent to the SCell with `drxConfig=Special DRX Config`.
5. **User Modify Response (SCell to UE)**: The SCell responds with `PsUser_UserModifyResp`.
6. **RRC Reconfiguration Check**: An alternative flow is introduced to check RRC Reconfiguration.
7. **Scenario 1: RRC Reconfiguration Succeeds**:
\* The UE sends `PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq` to the network with `transformPrecoderSwitchInd=success` and `drxConfigurationMode=modification`.
\* A sub-message `PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq` is sent to the SCell with `ndrxConfigurationMode=modification`.
\* The network applies the special DRX configuration. This is represented by two boxes: "(5) Apply Special DRX Config" and "(5.1) Apply Special DRX Config".
8. **Scenario 2: RRC Reconfiguration Fails**:
\* The UE sends `PsUser_UserModifyReq` to the network with `transformPrecoderSwitchAck=CANCELLATION` and `drxConfig=Previous DRX Profile2`.
\* A sub-message `PsUser_UserModifyReq` is sent to the SCell with `drxConfig=Previous DRX Profile2`.
\* The SCell responds with `PsUser_UserModifyResp`.
\* The UE sends `PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq` with `drxConfigurationMode=modification`.
\* The DRX configuration remains unchanged, indicated by "(8) DRX Config keep unchanged" and "(8.1) DRX Config keep unchanged".
The diagram uses standard UML sequence diagram notation with lifelines representing the participants and arrows representing messages exchanged between them. The text within the boxes describes the messages and their parameters.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_555.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

##### 6.1.8.2.1.2 Description:

###### 6.1.8.2.1.2.0-1 Description: General Description (ID: 11181249)

**6.1.8.2.1.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11181256`)

Description:
For general flowchart of User reconfiguration required indication please refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_132.

---

###### 6.1.8.2.1.2.0-2 Description: (2) PsUser_UserModifyReq (ID: 11181262)

**6.1.8.2.1.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11181270`)

Description:
In addition to the accept of the reconfiguration request(transformPrecoderSwitchAck=TRUE), the new DRX config shall be included and L2-PS will store this DRX config but will not apply it at once.

---

###### 6.1.8.2.1.2.0-3 Description: (2.1) and (2.2)  PsUser_UserModifyReq/ PsUser_UserModifyResp (ID: 11181275)

**6.1.8.2.1.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11181281`)

Description:
For Scell, the new DRX config shall be included in PsUser\_UserModifyReq and L2-PS will respond with PsUser\_UserModifyResq. L2-PS will store this DRX config but will not apply it at once.

---

###### 6.1.8.2.1.2.0-4 Description: (4) PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq (ID: 11181288)

**6.1.8.2.1.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11181294`)

Description:
In addtion to indicate successful RRC reconfiguration of TP switch ON, drxConfigMode is set to NewDrxDone meanning new DRX configuration has taken effects on UE side.

---

###### 6.1.8.2.1.2.0-5 Description: (4.1) PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq (ID: 11181301)

**6.1.8.2.1.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11181308`)

Description:
For SCell, drxConfigMode is set to NewDrxDone meanning new DRX configuration has taken effects on UE side.

---

###### 6.1.8.2.1.2.0-6 Description: (5) and (5.1) Apply Special DRX Config (ID: 11181314)

**6.1.8.2.1.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11181320`)

Description:
Now it is right time to apply new DRX config on L2-PS side

---

###### 6.1.8.2.1.2.0-7 Description: (7) PsUser_UserModifyReq (ID: 11181326)

**6.1.8.2.1.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11181333`)

Description:
In case RRCReconfiguration fails, the previous DRX Profile2 configuration will be included.

---

###### 6.1.8.2.1.2.0-8 Description: (7.1) PsUser_UserModifyReq and (7.2) PsUser_UserModifyResp (ID: 11181337)

**6.1.8.2.1.2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11181345`)

Description:
For Scell, in case RRCReconfiguration fails the previous DRX Profile2 configuration will be included in PsUser\_UserModifyReq and L2-PS needs to respond with PsUser\_UserModifyResp.

---

###### 6.1.8.2.1.2.0-9 Description: (8) and (8.1) DRX Config keeps unchanged (ID: 11181351)

**6.1.8.2.1.2.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11181358`)

Description:
Since RRCReconfiguration fails and new DRX Config will not take into effect on UE side. L2-PS will keep previous DRX configuration unchanged.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the process of exiting the SAG ON state and reverting to regular DRX configuration in a 5G network. The diagram depicts interactions between three entities: 5G-CP-RT, PCell (5G-L2-PS), and SCell (5G-L2-PS).
The diagram begins with the "SAG ON UE, Special DRX Config has been enabled" state.
The main flow involves the following steps:
1. **PsUser\_ReconfigurationRequiredInd**: Sent from 5G-CP-RT to PCell, indicating that reconfiguration is required and `TransformPrecoderInd` is set to `disabled`.
2. **PsUser\_UserModifyReq**: Sent from 5G-CP-RT to PCell with `transformPrecoderSwitchAck` set to `TRUE` and `drxConfig` set to `Regular DRX Config`.
\* **2.1 PsUser\_UserModifyReq**: Sent from PCell to SCell with `drxConfig` set to `RegularDRX Config`.
\* **2.2 PsUser\_UserModifyResp**: Sent from SCell to PCell.
3. **Apply Regular DRX Config**: A general action indicating the application of the regular DRX configuration.
\* **3.1 Apply Regular DRX Config**: Sent from PCell to SCell.
An alternative flow is presented under the "Alt Check RRCReconfiguration" section.
**Case 1: If RRCReconfiguration succeeds (4)**
5. **PsUser\_RrcReconfCompletedReq**: Sent from 5G-CP-RT to PCell with `transformPrecoderSwitchInd` set to `success` and `drxConfigurationMode` set to `modification`.
\* **5.1 PsUser\_RrcReconfCompletedReq**: Sent from PCell to SCell with `drxConfigurationMode` set to `modification`.
**Case 2: If RRCReconfiguration fails (6)**
7. **PsUser\_UserModifyReq**: Sent from 5G-CP-RT to PCell with `transformPrecoderSwitchAck` set to `CANCELLATION` and `drxConfig` set to `Previous Special DRX Config`.
\* **7.1 PsUser\_UserModifyReq**: Sent from PCell to SCell with `drxConfig` set to `Previous Special DRX Config`.
\* **7.2 PsUser\_UserModifyResp**: Sent from SCell to PCell.
\* **7.3 PsUser\_RrcReconfCompletedReq**: Sent from 5G-CP-RT to PCell with `drxConfigurationMode` set to `modification`.
8. **Restore Special DRX Config**: A general action indicating the restoration of the special DRX configuration.
\* **8.1 Restore Special DRX Config**: Sent from PCell to SCell.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_579.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

---

##### 6.1.8.2.2.2 Description:

###### 6.1.8.2.2.2.0-1 Description: General Description (ID: 11181412)

**6.1.8.2.2.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11181416`)

Description:
For general flowchart of User reconfiguration required indication please refer to 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_132.

---

###### 6.1.8.2.2.2.0-2 Description: (2) PsUser_UserModifyReq (ID: 11181423)

**6.1.8.2.2.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11181430`)

Description:
In addition to the accept of the reconfiguration request(transformPrecoderSwitchAck=TRUE), the new DRX config shall be included.

---

###### 6.1.8.2.2.2.0-3 Description: (2.1) and (2.2)  PsUser_UserModifyReq/ PsUser_UserModifyResp (ID: 11181436)

**6.1.8.2.2.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11181442`)

Description:
For Scell, the new DRX config shall be included in PsUser\_UserModifyReq and L2-PS will respond with PsUser\_UserModifyResq. L2-PS will store this DRX config but will not apply it at once.

---

###### 6.1.8.2.2.2.0-4 Description: (3) and (3.1) Apply Regular DRX Config (ID: 11181450)

**6.1.8.2.2.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11181456`)

Description:
Once receving new DRX Config, it will be applied at once.

---

###### 6.1.8.2.2.2.0-5 Description: (5) PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq (ID: 11181462)

**6.1.8.2.2.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11181468`)

Description:
In addtion to indicate successful RRC reconfiguration of TP switch ON, drxConfigMode is set to NewDrxDone meanning new DRX configuration has taken effects on UE side.

---

###### 6.1.8.2.2.2.0-6 Description: (5.1) PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq (ID: 11181475)

**6.1.8.2.2.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11181483`)

Description:
For SCell, drxConfigMode is set to NewDrxDone meanning new DRX configuration has taken effects on UE side.

---

###### 6.1.8.2.2.2.0-7 Description: (7) PsUser_UserModifyReq (ID: 11181490)

**6.1.8.2.2.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11181496`)

Description:
In case RRCReconfiguration fails, the previous Special DRX configuration will be included.

---

###### 6.1.8.2.2.2.0-8 Description: (7.1) PsUser_UserModifyReq and (7.2) PsUser_UserModifyResp (ID: 11181503)

**6.1.8.2.2.2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11181512`)

Description:
For Scell, in case RRCReconfiguration fails the previous Special DRX configuration will be included in PsUser\_UserModifyReq and L2-PS needs to respond with PsUser\_UserModifyResp.

---

###### 6.1.8.2.2.2.0-9 Description: (8) and (8.1)Restore Special DRX Config (ID: 11181519)

**6.1.8.2.2.2.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11181527`)

Description:
Since RRCReconfiguration fails but the new DRX Config has been applied in step (3). L2-PS will rollback and restore Special DRX config.

---

(NSA/SA) 11181554: User Setup in gNB-DU (NSA/SA) [image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "User Setup in gNB-DU (NSA/SA)" process. It depicts interactions between different components: "DU" (which is further divided into "5G-L2-PS", "5G-L2-LO", and "5G-L2-HIDU") and "5G C-Plane". The diagram shows the following sequence of events: 1. PsUser_UserSetupReq(User context, DRB, SRB1, SRB2) : This message is sent from the "5G C-Plane" to the "5G-L2-PS" component within the "DU". 2. A text box associated with the "5G-L2-PS" component states: "User and DRB, SRB setup in the target cell. 5G-L2-PS allocates C-RNTI and indicate it to C-Plane." This indicates that after receiving the request, the "5G-L2-PS" component performs user and DRB/SRB setup, allocates a C-RNTI, and informs the "5G C-Plane". 3. PsUser_UserSetupResp : This message is sent from the "5G-L2-PS" component back to the "5G C-Plane". 4. LoUser_UserSetupReq(User context, DRB, SRB1, SRB2) : This message is sent from the "5G C-Plane" to the "5G-L2-LO" component within the "DU". 5. A text box associated with the "5G-L2-LO" component states: "User and DRB, SRB setup in the target cell 5G-L2-LO." This indicates that after receiving the request, the "5G-L2-LO" component performs user and DRB/SRB setup in the target cell. The "5G-L2-HIDU" component is shown within the "DU" but does not appear to be directly involved in the depicted message flow.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m1dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_Flows_file_601.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] (ID: 11181554)

The diagram depicts interactions between different components within a "Primary gNB" and an "External gNB". The components are organized into two main sections: "Primary gNB" and "External gNB". Under "Primary gNB", the components are: - SCell 5G-L2-LO - L2-HI(DU) - MgNB-TRSW Under "External gNB", the components are: - SgNB-TRSW - SCell 5G-L2-LO The diagram shows several messages and actions exchanged between these components, numbered from (1) to (7). Here's a breakdown of the interactions: - (1) Alt : This indicates an alternative flow. - (2) Intra-gNB SCell : This is a labeled interaction within the gNB. - (3) LoData_UeDataDeliveryStatusInd (I2LoActivatedForData=True) : A message sent from SCell 5G-L2-LO (Primary gNB) to L2-HI(DU) (Primary gNB). A note indicates that "Local 5G-L2-LO sends the DDDS feedback message indication through LoData interface to the 5G-L2-HI". - Flow Control selects Local SCell for data transfer : An action occurring after message (3). - (4) LoData_DIDrbRlcPduSendReq : A message sent from L2-HI(DU) (Primary gNB) to SCell 5G-L2-LO (Primary gNB). - (5) Inter-gNB SCell : This is a labeled interaction between gNBs. - (6) XgU: DU DL DATA DELIVERY STATUS (I2LoActivatedForData=True) : A message sent from SCell 5G-L2-LO (External gNB) to MgNB-TRSW (Primary gNB). A note indicates that "Remote 5G-L2-LO sends the DU DL Data Delivery Status feedback message indication through TRSW/Xg-U to the 5G-L2-HI on primary gNB". - Flow Control selects Remote SCell for data transfer : An action occurring after message (6). - (7) XgU: DU DL USER DATA : A message sent from MgNB-TRSW (Primary gNB) to SgNB-TRSW (External gNB). A note indicates that "5G-L2-HI sends the DU DL User Data RLC PDU through TRSW/Xg-U to the 5G-L2-LO on external gNB". (4) LoData\_DlDrbRlcPduSendReq

Direction: 5G-L2-HI (DU) -> 5G-L2-LO (local)

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the process of SCell addition in gNB-DU for FR1. The diagram depicts interactions between different components: 5G-CP-RT, 5G-L2-PS, and gNB-DU for intra-gNB SA CA, prime-gNB-DU for inter-gNB SA CA, SgNB-DU for NSA CA, and ext-gNB-DU for inter-gNB SA CA.
The diagram is structured with vertical lifelines representing these components and horizontal arrows indicating messages exchanged between them. The messages are labeled with numbers and descriptions of the actions or conditions.
The diagram is divided into three main sections, each representing a different scenario or condition:
**Section 1 (Intra-gNB SCell addition in FR1 SA):**
\* **Preceding procedure:** User Setup in PCell in FR1 SA/NSA.
\* **Alt:** (1.1) Is the procedure intra-gNB SCell addition in FR1 SA?
\* **Opt:** (1.2) If Nr Rel is not yet established
\* **Ref:** (1.3) Nr Rel Setup in FR1 SA
\* Messages: (1.4) PsUser\_UserSetupReq, (1.5) PsUser\_UserSetupResp
\* **Ref:** (1.6) RRC Reconfiguration Complete Indicator in User Modify
**Section 2 (Inter-gNB ext-SCell addition in FR1 SA):**
\* **Alt:** (2.1) Is the procedure inter-gNB ext-SCell addition in FR1 SA?
\* **Opt:** (2.2) If Nr Rel is not yet established
\* **Ref:** (2.3) Nr Rel Setup in FR1 SA
\* Messages: (2.4) PsUser\_UserSetupReq, (2.5) PsUser\_UserSetupResp, (2.6) PsUser\_UserModifyReq, (2.7) PsUser\_UserModifyResp
\* **Ref:** (2.8) RRC Reconfiguration Complete Indicator in User Modify
**Section 3 (SCell addition in FR1 NSA):**
\* **Alt:** (3.1) Is the procedure SCell addition in FR1 NSA?
\* **Opt:** (3.2) If Nr Rel is not yet established
\* **Ref:** (3.3) Nr Rel Setup in FR1 SA
\* Messages: (3.4) PsUser\_UserSetupReq, (3.5) PsUser\_UserSetupResp
\* **Ref:** (3.6) RRC Reconfiguration Complete Indicator in User Modify

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating the process of SCell addition in gNB-DU for FR2. It depicts a sequence of interactions between different components.
The diagram is divided into two main sections, representing two alternative scenarios:
**Scenario 1 (Alt): SCell addition in FR2 SA**
\* This scenario is initiated by a question: "(1.1) Is the procedure Scell addition in FR2 SA?".
\* Following this, there are two referenced steps:
\* "(1.2) User Setup in FR2 SA"
\* "(1.3) SCell addition preparation in FR2 SA"
**Scenario 2: SCell addition in FR2 NSA**
\* This scenario is initiated by a question: "(2.1) Is the procedure Scell addition in FR2 NSA?".
\* This scenario involves a series of message exchanges between two entities, labeled "5G-L2-PS" and "5G-CP-RT", within the "gNB-DU" boundary. The messages are:
\* "(2.2) PsUser\_UserSetupReq" (sent from 5G-L2-PS to 5G-CP-RT)
\* "(2.3) PsUser\_UserSetupResp" (sent from 5G-CP-RT to 5G-L2-PS)
\* "(2.4) PsUser\_UserModifyReq" (sent from 5G-L2-PS to 5G-CP-RT)
\* "(2.5) PsUser\_UserModifyResp" (sent from 5G-CP-RT to 5G-L2-PS)
The diagram uses standard sequence diagram notation with lifelines representing the components and arrows indicating message flow. The "Alt" keyword signifies an alternative flow.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_665.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

##### 6.1.11.1.3.0-2 SCell addition preparation in FR2 Description (ID: 11182012)

**6.1.11.1.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11182019`)

SCell addition preparation in FR2
(1.1) Is the procedure SCell addition in FR2 SA?

---

**6.1.11.1.3.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11182024`)

SCell addition preparation in FR2
For SCell addition in FR2 SA, proceed with steps 1.2 (see 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_4138\_replaced([11182031](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BepDBvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and 1.3 (see 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_4140\_replaced([11182044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BepqAfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

**6.1.11.1.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11182031`)

SCell addition preparation in FR2
(1.2) User Setup in FR2 SA

---

**6.1.11.1.3.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11182038`)

SCell addition preparation in FR2
Preceding procedure (see 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_143\_replaced([11181541](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BenNyPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

In FR2 SA CA, 5G-L2-PS receives PsUser\_UserSetupReq with ueAddCause =InitialAccess (see  5G\_L2\_IF\_390\_replaced([10974651](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and configures only PCell.

---

**6.1.11.1.3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11182044`)

SCell addition preparation in FR2
(1.3) SCell addition preparation in FR2 SA

---

**6.1.11.1.3.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11182052`)

SCell addition preparation in FR2
5G-L2-PS proceeds with SCell addition procedure according to 5G\_L3\_FLOW\_79308 diagram and description in 5G\_L2\_12994\_replaced([11159879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25T7ofvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**6.1.11.1.3.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11182060`)

SCell addition preparation in FR2
(2.1) Is the procedure SCell addition in FR2 NSA?

---

**6.1.11.1.3.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11182067`)

SCell addition preparation in FR2
For SCell addition in FR2 NSA, proceed with step 2.2 (see 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_4144\_replaced([11182074](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BepqC_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

**6.1.11.1.3.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `11182074`)

SCell addition preparation in FR2
(2.2) PsUser\_UserSetupReq

---

**6.1.11.1.3.0-2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11182081`)

SCell addition preparation in FR2
5G-L2-PS receives PsUser\_UserSetupReq (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_390\_replaced([10974651](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with configuration for PScell and Scell(s)::

 UEAddCause = InitialAccessSgnbAddition,

 cellConfiguration IE, where index 0, corresponds to PSCell. Greater indexes correspond to SCell(s).

---

**6.1.11.1.3.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `11182086`)

SCell addition preparation in FR2
(2.3) PsUser\_UserSetupResp

---

**6.1.11.1.3.0-2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11182093`)

SCell addition preparation in FR2
5G-L2-PS responds with PsUser\_UserSetupResp (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_441\_replaced([10975908](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VDhZvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to 5G-CP-RT after user setup in SCell. For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_387\_replaced([10974588](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U8zv_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**6.1.11.1.3.0-2.0-7**  (ID: `11182100`)

SCell addition preparation in FR2
(2.4) PsUser\_UserModifyReq

---

**6.1.11.1.3.0-2.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `12802948`)

SCell addition preparation in FR2
5G-L2-PS receives PsUser\_UserModifyReq (see*5G\_L2\_IF\_453\_replaced([10976074](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VEvgvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with updated PSCell configuration:*

 *CellConfigurationForAddition and* ueAddCause are empty,\*\*

[Before CNI-134949-A]

 *CellConfigurationForModification is present and contains below parameters:*

o *numOfPerCsiReportConfig*

o *perCsiReportConfig*

[CNI-134949-A]

 *CellConfigurationForModification is present and contains below parameters:*

o *perCsiReportConfig*

[End CNI-134949-A]

**6.1.11.1.3.0-2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11182120`)

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating a process related to gNB (Next Generation NodeB) and SCell (Secondary Cell) management in a 5G network. The diagram depicts interactions between different components, including "ext-gNB for inter-gNB CA" with a "Secondary Cell" and "5G-L2-PS", and "gNB for intra-gNB CA / prime-gNB for inter-gNB CA" with a "Primary Cell" and "5G-L2-PS", "5G-L2-Hi(DU)", and "5G-CP-RT".
The sequence of events is as follows:
1. **(10) PsUser\_UserModifyReq**: A request is sent from the "gNB for intra-gNB CA / prime-gNB for inter-gNB CA" to the "ext-gNB for inter-gNB CA".
2. **(20) Buffer UserModifyReq**: The "ext-gNB for inter-gNB CA" buffers the received request.
3. **(30) Does the remote Scell To Release contain SCell(s) on ext-gNB?**: A decision point or query is made within the "ext-gNB for inter-gNB CA".
\* **(30.10) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq**: If the condition in step (30) is met, a request is sent from the "ext-gNB for inter-gNB CA" (specifically from the "Secondary Cell" component) to the "gNB for intra-gNB CA / prime-gNB for inter-gNB CA" (specifically to the "5G-L2-Hi(DU)" component).
\* **(30.20) SCell deactivation**: An action of "SCell deactivation" is performed within the "ext-gNB for inter-gNB CA".
\* **(30.30) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingResp**: A response is sent back from the "gNB for intra-gNB CA / prime-gNB for inter-gNB CA" (specifically from the "5G-L2-Hi(DU)" component) to the "ext-gNB for inter-gNB CA" (specifically to the "Secondary Cell" component).
4. **(40) PsUser\_UserModifyResp**: A response is sent from the "gNB for intra-gNB CA / prime-gNB for inter-gNB CA" to the "ext-gNB for inter-gNB CA".
5. **(50) Enter Transient Phase id UE capability change and Handle Transient**: The "gNB for intra-gNB CA / prime-gNB for inter-gNB CA" enters a transient phase for UE capability change and handling transient states.
6. **(60) PsUser\_RrcReconfCompleteReq**: A request is sent from the "gNB for intra-gNB CA / prime-gNB for inter-gNB CA" (specifically to the "5G-CP-RT" component).
7. **(70) Exit transient Phase after RRC complete**: The "gNB for intra-gNB CA / prime-gNB for inter-gNB CA" exits the transient phase after RRC (Radio Resource Control) completion.
The diagram also includes a reference "Ref IGNB CA SCell Release Preparation in prime-gNB-DU" and a footer with a URL: "http:/msc-generator.sourceforge.net v8.3.7". The "Opt" label next to the "ext-gNB for inter-gNB CA" line suggests that some of the interactions might be optional.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_709.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating a communication protocol. The diagram depicts interactions between different components, labeled as "5G-L2-PS", "5G-L2-LO", "5G-L2-Hi(DU)", and "5G-CP-RT". These components are organized within larger functional blocks: "Secondary Cell for intra- or inter-gB CA" and "gNB-DU for intra-gB CA" / "ext-gNB-DU for inter-gB CA".
The diagram shows several messages exchanged between these components, indicated by arrows and text labels. The messages are numbered and include:

**6.1.13.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11182363`)

Scell Release in Intra- and Inter-gNB CA

---

**6.1.13.0-3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11182377`)

Scell Release in Intra- and Inter-gNB CA
[CNI-84537-A]

Direction: PCell 5G-CP-RT -> PCell 5G-L2-PS

Message definition: 5G\_L2\_IF\_453\_replaced([10976074](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VEvgvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Upon reception of the PsUser\_UserModifyReq for Scell release message from CPRT,

1. For Pcell 5G-L2-PS

1.1. Buffer PsUser\_UserModifyReq, and handle message after N=2 DPA scheduler cycles delay (A DPA scheduler cycle corresponding to rdSchedulePUCCHCycle\_msec)

1.2. For transient phase handling, enter only if UE’s parameter in PsUser\_UserModifyReq change, and exit when receiving PsUser\_RrcReconfCompletedReq for Scell release.

1.3. For more handling details, refer to 5G\_L2\_2872\_replaced([11160006](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25UiufvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

1. For Scell 5G-L2-PS, it shall stop scheduling of the UE.

[END CNI-84537-A]

The diagram is divided into several phases: "Preparation Phase" and "RRC Completion Phase". Within these phases, messages are exchanged between "PCell\_Sgnl", "PCell\_PS", "PCell\_DL", "PCell\_UL", "SCell\_Sgnl", "SCell\_PS\_dl\_ul", "SCell\_DL", "SCell\_UL", and "CP".
**Preparation Phase:**
\* "PsUser\_UserModifyReq" is sent from "PCell\_Sgnl" to "PCell\_DL".
\* "PsUser\_UserModifyReq" is then sent from "PCell\_DL" to "SCell\_DL".
\* Message 1: "PsUser\_UserModifyReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_453) with ScellRelease" is sent from "SCell\_DL" to "SCell\_PS\_dl\_ul".
\* Message 2: "PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUIBufferSplitInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_2147) (rrmBufferedDataUITotalBytes=0, ifHarqNeedClear=TRUE)" is sent from "SCell\_PS\_dl\_ul" to "SCell\_DL".
\* Message 3: "PsUser\_UserModifyResp (5G\_L2\_IF\_458)" is sent from "SCell\_DL" to "SCell\_PS\_dl\_ul".
Following this, there's a highlighted section labeled "Release SCell RRC".
**RRC Completion Phase:**
\* Message 8: "PsUser\_RrcReconfCompleteReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_2575)" is sent from "PCell\_Sgnl" to "PCell\_DL".
\* "PsUser\_RrcReconfCompleteReq" is then sent from "PCell\_DL" to "SCell\_DL".
A separate section labeled "Delete Scell UE context" shows further interactions:
\* Message 4: "PsUser\_UserStopReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_2569)" is sent from "SCell\_DL" to "SCell\_PS\_dl\_ul".
\* "PsUser\_UserStopReq" is then sent from "SCell\_PS\_dl\_ul" to "SCell\_DL".
\* Message 5: "PsUser\_UserStopResp (5G\_L2\_IF\_2554)" is sent from "SCell\_DL" to "SCell\_PS\_dl\_ul".
\* Message 6: "PsUser\_UserDeleteReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_473)" is sent from "SCell\_PS\_dl\_ul" to "SCell\_DL".
\* "PsUser\_UserDeleteReq" is then sent from "SCell\_DL" to "SCell\_PS\_dl\_ul".
\* Message 7: "PsUser\_UserDeleteResp (5G\_L2\_IF\_474)" is sent from "SCell\_PS\_dl\_ul" to "SCell\_DL".

#### 6.1.14.1.0-2 SCell (DL+UL) release Description (ID: 11182686)

**6.1.14.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11182692`)

SCell (DL+UL) release
When releasing SCell is a CA UE’s DL/UL SCell, after PCell receives the msg in step1, delays handling this msg(refer to 5G\_L2\_16303\_replaced([11158861](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25NN9_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then:

1) PCell should recycle the unscheduled data buffer splitted to Scell;

2) PCell should stop the buffer split algorithm;

3) PCell sends rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes=0 to SCell to stop UL scheduling in SCell UL by msg PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_2147\_replaced([10980201](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vg0Zfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

4) PCell sends ifHarqNeedClear=TRUE to SCell by msg PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd, for the scheduling UL harq in SCell, if the feedback is not Ack, the harq's retransmit num should be set to the Max Retransmit Num, the harq will be released by harq process;

5) Scell UL deletes UE context after receiving msg PsUser\_UserDeleteReq.

---

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "Scell(DLOnly) Release" process. The diagram is divided into three phases: Preparation Phase, DLOnly Scell Release, and Completion Phase.
The diagram depicts interactions between different entities, including PCell (PS, DL, UL), SCell1 (Sgnl, DL, UL), SCell2 (Sgnl, DL, UL), and CP.
**Preparation Phase:**
- PsUser\_UserModifyReq is sent from PCell\_PS to SCell1\_DL.
- PsUser\_UserModifyReq is sent from PCell\_PS to SCell1\_UL.
- Message 1: PsUser\_UserModifyReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_447) with Scell Release is sent from PCell\_PS to SCell1\_DL.
- Message 2: PsPeerCtrl\_PcellCsiStatusInd (Release+TransientStart) is sent from SCell1\_DL to SCell2\_DL.
- Message 3: PsUser\_UserModifyResp (5G\_L2\_IF\_447) is sent from SCell1\_DL to PCell\_PS.
**DLOnly Scell Release:**
- Message 4: PsUser\_UserStopReq is sent from SCell1\_DL to SCell1\_Sgnl.
- PsUser\_UserStopReq is sent from SCell1\_Sgnl to SCell1\_DL.
- Message 5: PsUser\_UserStopResp is sent from SCell1\_DL to SCell1\_Sgnl.
- Message 6: PsUser\_UserDeleteReq is sent from SCell1\_DL to SCell1\_Sgnl.
- PsUser\_UserDeleteReq is sent from SCell1\_Sgnl to SCell1\_DL.
- Message 7: PsUser\_UserDeleteResp is sent from SCell1\_DL to SCell1\_Sgnl.
- A yellow bar indicates "Release SCell1 RRC".
**Completion Phase:**
- PsUser\_RrcReconfCompleteReq is sent from PCell\_PS to SCell1\_DL.
- PsUser\_RrcReconfCompleteReq is sent from PCell\_PS to SCell1\_UL.
- Message 8: PsUser\_RrcReconfCompleteReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_542) is sent from PCell\_PS to SCell1\_DL.
- Message 9: PsPeerCtrl\_PcellCsiStatusInd (Release+TransientStop) is sent from SCell1\_DL to SCell2\_DL.

[CNI-136896-A]
[image-1][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "Scell(DLOnly) Release" process. The diagram depicts interactions between different components, labeled as PCell\_Sgnl, PCell\_PS, PCell\_DL, PCell\_UL, SCell1\_Sgnl, SCell1\_DL, SCell1\_UL, SCell2\_Sgnl, SCell2\_DL, SCell2\_UL, and CP.
The process is divided into two main phases: "Preparation Phase" and "Completion Phase".
**Preparation Phase:**
- PCell\_Sgnl sends a "PsUser\_UserModifyReq" to PCell\_DL.
- PCell\_DL sends a "PsUser\_UserModifyReq" to SCell1\_DL.
- SCell1\_DL sends a "1. PsUser\_UserModifyReq(5G\_L2\_IF\_447) with Scell Release" to SCell1\_DL.
- SCell1\_DL sends a "2. psPeerCtrl\_PcellCsiStatusInd (Release+TransientStart)" to SCell2\_DL.
- SCell1\_DL sends a "3. PsUser\_UserModifyResp (5G\_L2\_IF\_447)" to PCell\_DL.
**Release SCell1 RRC:** This is a distinct phase indicated by a yellow bar.
**Completion Phase:**
- PCell\_Sgnl sends a "PsUser\_RrcReconfCompleteReq" to PCell\_DL.
- PCell\_DL sends a "4. PsUser\_RrcReconfCompleteReq(5G\_L2\_IF\_542)" to SCell1\_DL.
- SCell1\_DL sends a "5.psPeerCtrl\_PcellCsiStatusInd (Release+TransientStop)" to SCell2\_DL.
Following the "Completion Phase", there is a section labeled "DLOnly Scell Release" which details further interactions:
- SCell1\_Sgnl sends a "PsUser\_UserStopReq" to SCell1\_DL.
- SCell1\_DL sends a "6. PsUser\_UserStopReq" to SCell2\_DL.
- SCell1\_DL sends a "PsUser\_UserStopReq" to SCell2\_DL.
- SCell2\_DL sends a "7. PsUser\_UserStopResp" to SCell1\_DL.
- SCell1\_DL sends a "PsUser\_UserDeleteReq" to SCell1\_DL.
- SCell1\_DL sends a "8. PsUser\_UserDeleteReq" to SCell2\_DL.
- SCell1\_DL sends a "PsUser\_UserDeleteReq" to SCell2\_DL.
- SCell2\_DL sends a "9. PsUser\_UserDeleteResp" to SCell1\_DL.
The diagram also includes a URL at the bottom right: "https://gitlab.com/msc-generator v8.5".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-01151534.png[/image\_path][/image-1]
[End CNI-136896-A]
[Before CNI-136896-A]
File "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_4531\_Scell\_release\_dlOnly\_(3cc).signalling" stored at:
[CNI-136896-A]
File "13358934-A Scell release dlOnly (3cc).signalling" stored at:
[End CNI-136896-A]
 
Note: For DPA suspend and resume, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22730\_replaced([11123985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqnMA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 6.1.14.2.0-2 Scell (DL only) release under DL+UL CA Description (ID: 11182724)

**6.1.14.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11182730`)

Scell (DL only) release under DL+UL CA
For L2 PS, in Preparation Phase, PCell PS receives the PsUser\_UserModify msg with (size of remoteSCellToAddList, size of remoteScellToRelease)=(0,1) and the releasing SCell is a DLOnly SCell,

PCell shall send the CSI of the releasing SCell with (cause=Release and status=TransientStart) to the UL/DL SCell by msg psPeerCtrl\_PcellCsiStatusInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_2339\_replaced([10980559](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VjQqvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The UL/DL SCell receiving the msg and mark the received CSI to Transient state, which will lead the SCell UL can't be scheduled on the slot of these CSI.

In complete phase, PCell receive the msg PsUser\_RrcReconfCompleteReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_542\_replaced([10977666](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VN5fPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), PCell should send the CSI of the releasing SCell with (cause=Release and status=TransientStop) to the UL/DL SCell by msg PsPeerCtrl\_PcellCsiStatusInd.

The UL/DL SCell receiving the msg and clear these CSI.

---

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating "User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA". It depicts interactions between different network entities.
The entities involved are:
- PCell 5G-CP-RT
- PCell 5G-L2-PS
- SCell 5G-L2-PS
- ext-SCell 5G-L2-PS
These entities are grouped under different contexts:
- "gNB for intra-gNB CA" and "prime-gNB for inter-gNB CA" encompass PCell 5G-CP-RT, PCell 5G-L2-PS, and SCell 5G-L2-PS.
- "Text-gNB for inter-gNB CA" encompasses ext-SCell 5G-L2-PS.
The sequence of messages exchanged is as follows:
1. **(10) PsUser\_UserStopReq**: Sent from PCell 5G-CP-RT to PCell 5G-L2-PS.
2. **(20) Alt**: This is an alternative block initiated by PCell 5G-L2-PS. It presents three possible scenarios:
\* **(20.10) cause="handover"**: A message indicating a handover.
\* **(20.20) cause="release"**: A message indicating a release.
\* **(20.30) cause="s cell ReleaseStarf"**: A message indicating the start of cell release.
3. **(20.40) cause="interGnbCaUeRelease"**: A message indicating the release of UE in inter-gNB CA, sent from PCell 5G-L2-PS to SCell 5G-L2-PS.
\* **(20.40.10) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq (modifType="deactivateExtScell")**: Sent from SCell 5G-L2-PS to ext-SCell 5G-L2-PS, requesting SCell UE scheduling modification to deactivate the external SCell.
\* **(20.40.20) SCell deactivation**: An action or status related to SCell deactivation, associated with the message from SCell 5G-L2-PS to ext-SCell 5G-L2-PS.
\* **(20.40.30) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingResp**: A response to the scheduling request, sent from ext-SCell 5G-L2-PS back to SCell 5G-L2-PS.
4. **(30) PsUser\_UserStopResp**: Sent from SCell 5G-L2-PS back to PCell 5G-CP-RT, indicating the user stop response.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_778.002.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
Link to the "5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1765\_User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA.signalling" file:
**[CB009103-D]**
[image-1][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating a "User Stop" scenario in intra- and inter-gNB Carrier Aggregation (CA).
The diagram depicts interactions between different network entities:
- **PCell 5G-CP-RT**: Primary Cell for Control Plane Real-Time.
- **PCell 5G-L2-PS**: Primary Cell for Layer 2 Packet Switched.
- **SCell 5G-L2-PS**: Secondary Cell for Layer 2 Packet Switched.
- **ext-SCell 5G-L2-PS**: Secondary Cell for an external gNB, for inter-gNB CA.
The diagram is organized into sections representing different scenarios:
- **gNB for intra-gNB CA**: This section covers scenarios within a single gNB.
- **prime-gNB for inter-gNB CA**: This section covers scenarios for the primary gNB in inter-gNB CA.
- **Text-gNB for inter-gNB CA**: This section covers scenarios for the secondary (external) gNB in inter-gNB CA.
Key messages and events shown in the diagram include:
1. **(10) PsUser\_UserStopReq**: A request from the User Plane to stop the user session. This message is sent from PCell 5G-CP-RT to PCell 5G-L2-PS.
2. **(20) Alt**: This indicates an alternative flow.
\* **(20.10) cause="handover"**: A possible cause for the user stop.
\* **(20.20) cause="release"**: Another possible cause for the user stop.
\* **(20.30) cause="s cell ReleaseStart"**: A specific event related to the start of SCell release.
3. **(20.40) cause="interGnbCaUeRelease"**: A message indicating the release of the UE in inter-gNB CA. This message is sent from PCell 5G-L2-PS to SCell 5G-L2-PS.
4. **(20.40.10) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq(modifType="deactivateExtScell")**: A request to the peer control plane to deactivate the external SCell. This message is sent from PCell 5G-L2-PS to ext-SCell 5G-L2-PS.
5. **(20.40.20) SCell deactivation**: The ext-SCell 5G-L2-PS performs SCell deactivation.
6. **(20.40.30) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingResp**: A response to the SCell scheduling request. This message is sent from ext-SCell 5G-L2-PS back to PCell 5G-L2-PS.
7. **(20.50) Opt**: This indicates an optional flow.
\* **(20.50.10) Is intra-gNB SCell established?**: A question to check if an intra-gNB SCell is established. This is a decision point.
\* **(20.50.20) cause=release**: If the intra-gNB SCell is established, the cause is release.
8. **(30) PsUser\_UserStopResp**: A response from the User Plane indicating that the user stop process is complete. This message is sent from PCell 5G-L2-PS back to PCell 5G-CP-RT.
The diagram also includes a footer with the text "http://msc-generator.sourceforge.net v6.3.7".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/12536532\_User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

### 6.1.16.0-2 User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA Description: (ID: 11182789)

**6.1.16.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11182795`)

User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA
(10) PsUser\_UserStopReq

Message definition: 5G\_L2\_IF\_2569\_replaced([10976632](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VHy0fu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**6.1.16.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11182802`)

User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA
5G-CP-RT shall send PsUser\_UserStopReq to stop UE scheduling.

**6.1.16.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11182809`)

User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA
(20) Alternative

---

**6.1.16.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11182815`)

User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA
PCell 5G-L2-PS checks cause value received in PsUser\_UserStopReq message. [Before CNI-80481-B]If cause is set to interGnbCaUeRelease proceed with step 30. Otherwise proceed with step 50.[End CNI-80481-B]

(20.10) cause=”handover”

(20.20) cause=”release”

User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA
Legacy cause for intra-gNB CA.

(20.30) cause=”scellReleaseStart”

User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA

**6.1.16.0-2.0-10**  (ID: `12552299`)

User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA
(20.50.10) Is intra-gNB SCell established?

---

**6.1.16.0-2.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `12552308`)

User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA
If at least one SCell is established for related PCell in intra-gNB relation, then the PCell’s 5G-L2-PS shall proceed with step 20.50.20 (see [12552309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_3x--kCTcEfCNjfqfyUlvmw)).

---

**6.1.16.0-2.0-11**  (ID: `12552309`)

User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA
(20.50.20) cause = release

---

**6.1.16.0-2.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `12552312`)

User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA
When PCell’s 5G-L2-PS receives PsUser\_UserStopReq message (see [10976632](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_vg8bMPu4Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with cause IE equal to interGnbCaUeRelease and at least one intra-gNB SCell is established for this PCell (condition at step 20.50.10, see [12552299](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_drevwCTcEfCNjfqfyUlvmw)), then the PCell’s 5G-L2-PS shall proceed with intra-gNB SCell Stop procedure as for cause IE equal to release, see [11145254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_szSngPvLEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for more details.

---

User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA

---

**6.1.16.0-2.0-12.0-1**  (ID: `11182921`)

User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA
PCell 5G-L2-PS replies with PsUser\_UserStopResp.

### 6.1.16.0-3 User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA Exceptions (ID: 11182927)

Error case

**6.1.16.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11182941`)

User Stop in intra- and inter-gNB CA
If inter-gNB CA/SCell relation does not exist, PCell 5G-L2-PS shall not send the PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq message to SCell 5G-L2-PS.

3. A message labeled "(2) PsUser\_UserDeleteResp" is sent back from the gNB-DU (specifically from the "5G-CP-RT" component) to the "Ref" lifeline. This is indicated by an arrow pointing from the gNB-DU to "Ref".

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the "User Suspend Scheduling in intra- and inter-gNB CA". The diagram depicts interactions between different network entities: PCell 5G-CP-RT, PCell 5G-L2-PS, SCell 5G-L2-PS, and ext-SCell 5G-L2-PS.
The diagram shows the following sequence of messages:
1. **(10) PsUser\_UserSuspendSchedulingReq**: This is the initial request sent from the PCell 5G-CP-RT.
2. **(20) Alt**: This indicates an alternative flow. Within this alternative, several `ueSuspendCause` messages are shown, each representing a different reason for suspending the user:
\* **(20.10) ueSuspendCause="RRCReEstablishment"**: Suspend due to RRC Re-establishment.
\* **(20.20) ueSuspendCause="HO\_intra\_du"**: Suspend due to intra-gNB Handover.
\* **(20.30) ueSuspendCause="SgNBRelease"**: Suspend due to SgNB Release.
\* **(20.40) ueSuspendCause="HO\_others"**: Suspend due to other Handover reasons.
\* **(20.50) ueSuspendCause="HO\_with\_ExtScell"**: Suspend due to Handover with an external SCell.
3. **(20.50.10) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq(modifType="deactivateExtScell")**: This message is sent to the SCell 5G-L2-PS, requesting to deactivate the external SCell.
4. **(20.50.20) SCell deactivation**: This is a response or indication of SCell deactivation.
5. **(20.50.30) PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingResp**: This is a response to the `PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq` message.
6. **Opt**: This indicates an optional flow.
\* **(20.50.40) Is intra-gNB SCell established?**: A question to check if the intra-gNB SCell is established.
\* **(20.50.50) Proceed as for ueSuspendCause="HO\_intra\_du"**: If the intra-gNB SCell is established, proceed as per the "HO\_intra\_du" cause.
7. **(30) PsUser\_UserSuspendSchedulingResp**: This is the final response to the initial request, sent back to the PCell 5G-CP-RT.
The diagram is organized into sections representing different gNB configurations: "gNB for intra-gNB CA prime-gNB for inter-gNB CA" and "Text-gNB for inter-gNB CA". The overall title of the diagram is "User Suspend Scheduling in intra- and inter-gNB CA". [image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating the evaluation of DL/UL buffer status for SCell addition. The flowchart depicts interactions between different components, likely within a 5G network.
The main components identified are:
- **5G-L2-PS**: Likely a protocol stack layer or function.
- **gNB\_DU**: Represents the gNB Distributed Unit.
- **5G-CP-RT**: Likely a control plane real-time component.
The flowchart shows a sequence of events and messages exchanged between these components.
**Key events and messages:**
1. **(1.1) PsUser\_BufferMonitoringInd::start (5G\_L2\_IF\_4539)**: A request to start buffer monitoring is initiated.
2. **(1.2) Starting DL or UL or (DL and UL) buffer status monitoring (DL:5G\_UP\_ALG\_15832, UL:12639254)**: This indicates the initiation of buffer status monitoring for Downlink (DL), Uplink (UL), or both, with specific identifiers.
3. **(1.3) PsUser\_BufferMonitoringInd::start (5G\_L2\_IF\_4539)**: Another instance of the start monitoring request.
4. **(1.4) The request shall be ignored and P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall continue the monitoring without restarting**: This describes a condition where a request is disregarded, and the monitoring continues.
5. **(1.5) DL or UL buffer criterion for SCell Addition is met (DL:5G\_UP\_ALG\_15838, UL:12639251)**: This signifies that a condition related to buffer status for SCell addition has been met.
6. **(1.6) PsUser\_BufferCriterionInd (5G\_L2\_IF\_4540)**: An indication that a buffer criterion has been met.
7. **(1.7) Stop DL or UL buffer status monitoring based on BufferCriterionInd DL or UL respectively**: This indicates the stopping of buffer monitoring based on the criterion indication.
8. **(2.1) PsUser\_BufferMonitoringInd::stop (5G\_L2\_IF\_4539)**: A request to stop buffer monitoring.
9. **(2.2) Stop applicable for DL: The request shall be ignored if BufferCriterionInd for DL is already sent**: This describes a specific scenario for stopping DL monitoring, where the request is ignored if the DL criterion has already been signaled.
The flowchart uses rectangular boxes for messages/events and rounded rectangles for conditions or states. The "Opt" labels suggest optional paths or conditions. The cyan colored boxes likely represent specific processes or states within the system. The overall diagram is clear and well-structured, depicting a logical flow of operations.

The request shall be ignored and P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall continue the monitoring without restarting the internal counters related to the monitoring algorithm.

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the UE reconfiguration process during a step-wise SCell addition for a CA (Carrier Aggregation) UE. The diagram depicts interactions between different entities: PCell-L2-PS, SCell\_1-L2-PS, and 5G-CP-RT.
Here's a breakdown of the interactions:
1. **Initial State:** The diagram starts with the UE being in CA with a PCell and at least one SCell, and a new SCell is being added.
2. **Adding SCell:** The process begins with an option to add an SCell, which can be a specific type (5G\_L2\_21541) or not.
3. **User Modification Request:** A `PsUser_UserModifyReq` message is sent to add the SCell and reconfigure PCell parameters.
4. **Stop DPA and Delay:** The UE stops DPA (Data Path Activation) and delays NxDPA periods.
5. **User Modification Response:** A `PsUser_UserModifyResp` message is received.
6. **Transient Phase Handling:**
\* A condition is checked for a transient phase caused by specific 5G UP ALG values (4816, 8181, 4826, 4196).
\* If the transient phase is detected, the PCell schedule is adjusted based on the reconfigured parameters.
7. **SCell Status Check (UL CA CC):**
\* An alternative path (`alt`) is shown, checking if the existing SCell is a UL CA CC.
8. **UL SCell Active/Inactive Scenarios:**
\* **If UL SCell is active:**
\* A `PsPeerCtrl_PcellUIBufferSplitInd` message is sent, indicating a stop in split buffer to SCell.
\* A condition `(1.6)SCell has no data for UL scheduling` is noted.
\* **If UL SCell is not active:**
\* A condition `(1.7)if Scell is activated during step-wise scell addition procedure, no UL data split to Scell before RRC complete` is described.
9. **RRC Reconfiguration Completion:** A `PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq` message is sent.
10. **PCSI/BM Report Change:**
\* An optional condition is checked: if the number of bits for existing PCSI report or beam report for PCell or retained SCell may change according to specific 5G UP ALG values (12845) and if the existing DL-UL SCell is not for T+F UL CA.
\* If the condition is met, a `PsPeerCtrl_PcellCsiStatusind` message is sent to inform the DL-UL SCell about PCell's/active SCell's P-CSI/BM report change.
11. **End Transient Phase:**
\* The transient phase ends, and DPA is started.
12. **UL Buffer Split:**
\* An optional condition is checked: if the existing UL SCell is active and PCell has UL buffer to split.
\* If true, UL buffer split is started again.
The diagram also includes a footer with a URL: `http:/msc-generator.sourceforge.net v3.3.7`.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m1dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_Flows\_file\_891.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
flow chart link:

#### 6.1.19.3.0-2 UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE Description: (ID: 11183553)

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11183560`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
(1.1) PsUser\_UserModifyReq

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11183565`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
Direction: 5G-CP-RT -> 5G-L2-PS

Message definition: 5G\_L2\_IF\_5165\_replaced([10976067](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VEvgfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

5G-CP-RT shall send PsUser\_UserModifyReq to 5G-L2-PS to inform PCell about SCell addition. Along with the SCell addition, PCell's L1 parameter may be configured or not configured.

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11183574`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
(1.2)Stop DPA and delay NxDPA

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11183580`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
When a CA UE is reconfigured, if its SCell is active it may be being scheduled with DPA resource as 5G\_L2\_589\_replaced([11158134](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25Jjm_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), so stop the DPA and delay NxDPA periods as 5G\_L2\_16303\_replaced([11158861](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25NN9_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to guarantee that its possible allocated PUCCH resource allocated by DPA can be used out by DL scheduling.

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11183585`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
(1.3) PsUser\_UserModifyResp

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11183593`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
Direction: 5G-L2-PS->5G-CP-RT

Message definition: 5G\_L2\_IF\_5164\_replaced([10976511](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VGkw_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

5G-L2-PS send response to 5G-CP-RT about the user modification requested by previous PsUser\_UserModifyReq. This message is sent out on the slot when 5G-L2-PS delay NxDPA periods after receiving PsUser\_UserModifyReq as (1.2) in 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_6137\_replaced([11183574](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeyM4PvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11183599`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
(1.4)enter transient phase

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11183606`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
When UE is reconfigured by high layer RRC reconfiguration, before receiving UE's RRC reconfiguration complete message, 5G-L2-PS should not take the reconfigured parameter into usage, neither use the legacy parameter before configuration. So UE's scheduling enter transient phase to use corresponding default value of the parameter, scheduling behavior in transient phase depends on the reconfigured parameter. The possible reconfiguration may for PCell or for SCell's PCSI/BM report.

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `11183613`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
(1.5)PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd with stop split buffer to SCell

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11183619`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
Direction: PCell 5G-L2-PS->SCell 5G-L2-PS

If the PsUser\_UserModifyReq is not for only SCell addition, if there is DL+UL SCell in existing SCells, PCell send PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd to stop the UL buffer split to the UL SCell.

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `11183625`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
(1.6)SCell has no data for UL scheduling

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11183632`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
Upon receiving PsPeerCtrl\_PcellUlBufferSplitInd to stop the UL buffer split, SCell will stop UL scheduling due to no data to schedule.

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-7**  (ID: `11183638`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
(1.7)if Scell is activated during step-wise scell addition procedure

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11183643`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
If Scell is activated during step-wise scell addition procedure, PCell should not trigger UL data split to Scell before RRC complete.

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-8**  (ID: `11183649`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
(1.8) PsUser\_RrcReconfCompletedReq

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11183656`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
Direction: 5G-CP-RT->5G-L2-PS

Message definition: 5G\_L2\_IF\_542\_replaced([10977666](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VN5fPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

5G-CP-RT send this message to inform 5G-L2-PS the user reconfiguration process started from PsUser\_UserModifyReq is complete, the added SCell and reconfigured parameter can be taken into usage.

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-9**  (ID: `11183666`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
(1.9) PsPeerCtrl\_PCellCsiStatusInd

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11183671`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
Direction: PCell 5G-L2-PS DL->SCell 5G-L2-PS UL

For F+T or F+F or T+T UL CA(see note), to inform the existing UL SCell about the changed for PCell's PCSI or beam report with different number of report bit without transient phase, so UL SCell can use the information for its PUSCH scheduling. [CB006139-DA] When a retained SCell's PCSI/BM report bit number is impacted and may change by the reconfiguration as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12845\_replaced([11159141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktHtdPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the information to active DL-UL SCell by the message PsPeerCtrl\_PCellCsiStatusInd needs only be done if the SCell is active. If the SCell is in active transient phase, then the message is not needed, the handling is as 5G\_L2\_22201\_replaced([11145986](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24CwW_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[End CB006139-DA]

Note:For F+T or F+F or T+T UL CA, the TDD DL+UL SCell may schedule PUSCH with PCSI if no scheduling on FDD PCell; but for T+F UL CA, on the overlap UL slots of TDD PCell and FDD SCell, either there is no UL scheduling on FDD SCell or TDD PCell shall schedule PUSCH mandatorily, the PCSI will not be on SCell PUSCH, so no need to pass the PCSI info to FDD SCell.

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-10**  (ID: `11183679`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
(1.10) end transient phase and start DPA

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `11183686`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
After PsUser\_RrcReconfCompletedReq is recieved from 5G\_CP\_RT, 5G\_L2\_PS is confirmed that the RRC reconfiguration is done and the possible reconfigured parameter can be taken into usage so the transient phase ends and the DPA allocating PUCCH for the CA UE can be restarted with UE's DCI1\_1 scheduling.

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-11**  (ID: `11183694`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
(1.11)Start UL Buffer split again

---

**6.1.19.3.0-2.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `11183700`)

UE Reconfiguration When Step-wise Buffer Based SCell Addition for CA UE
When the reconfiguration is completed, the UL buffer split should be re-started again if there is active UL SCell.

---
