### 6.1.30.0-2 Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG Descritpion (ID: 13415688)

**6.1.30.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13415710`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(1) Pcell 5G-L2-PS requests Timing Alignment procedure on SCell

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13415711`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
PCell sends PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq to SCell (message definition: [10979437: PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_D6EQcPu5Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Overview of procedure can be found in [13414170: UL Timing Alignment for SCells in Different TAG](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_QPSsZBLqEfG3gf_qmG8Vww).

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13415712`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(2) SCell 5G-L2-PS starts timer for procedure expiry

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13415713`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
SCell 5G-L2-PS starts timer at expiry of which Timing Alignment procedure will be considered failed (see steps 19, 20, 21). Timer depends on number fo retries of preamble transmissions UE can perform before abandoning scenario. For exact value see: [13414220: Timing Alignment for SCell with Different TAG procedure timeout calculation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_HCt11RLvEfG3gf_qmG8Vww);

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13415714`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(3) SCell 5G-L2-PS requests preamble from 5G-CP-RT

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13415715`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
5G-L2-PS requests CFRA preamble which will be used for PDCCH order procedure. Message definition: [13381573: PsUser\_ReserveCfraPreambleReq](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_WPBzeQAhEfGhFrIQm2O4Ew).

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `13415716`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(4) 5G-CP-RT reserves preamble

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13415717`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
5G-CP-RT tries to choose preamble from pool assigned for CFRA procedures. This pool can be exhausted (by other reserve requests or HO procedures). In such case 5G-CP-RT reponds with failure (status EStatus5G\_NotOk) which causes failure of Timing Alignment procedure (see steps: 18). Otherwise valid preamble is assigned and 5G-L2-PS can continue scenario. Message definition: [13381581: PsUser\_ReserveCfraPreambleResp](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_r36AYgAhEfGhFrIQm2O4Ew).

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `13415718`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(5) 5G-L2-PS sends PDCCH order

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `13415719`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
5G-L2-PS sends PDCCH order as DCI 1\_0 with format as per: [13353948: DCI Format 1\_0 structure to be Used for PDCCH Order](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_oTFAkO9_EfC3ocOh_n7w7A). This will trigger UE to perform CFRA preamble transmission.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `13415720`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(6) 5G-L1 transmits PDCCH with DCI

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `13415721`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
DCI is transmitted as scheduled by 5G-L2-PS. CFRA procedure is started at UE side.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-7**  (ID: `13415722`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(7) 5G-L2-PS schedules preamble reception

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `13415723`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
5G-L2-PS requests 5G-L1 to receive preamble (this is repetitive action not directly triggered by this procedure, however included here for consistency, if preamble is not received in following steps, this is repeated).

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-8**  (ID: `13415724`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(8) UE transmits RA preamble

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `13415725`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
UE transmits preamble with Id got from PDCCH order DCI in occasion associated with best SSB beam .

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-9**  (ID: `13415726`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(9) 5G-L1 notifies 5G-L2-PS about received preamble.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `13415727`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
5G-L1 sends UlData\_PrachReceiveInd to 5G-L2-PS.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-10**  (ID: `13415728`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(10) SCell 5G-L2-PS requests transmission of Random Access Response

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `13415729`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
SCell 5G-L2-PS sends PsPeerCtrl\_ScellRequestRarTransmissionInd (see: [13409064: PsPeerCtrl\_ScellRequestRarTransmissionInd](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_M1xxRg5oEfGu_4itz1o3RA)) request contains information which would be used to transmit Random Access Response by SCell itself. Only difference is TDRA which is sent as list of SLIV's mapped to k2 values, so that PCell is able to select slot for RAR transmission for requested MSG3 slot.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-11**  (ID: `13415730`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(11) SCell 5G-L2-PS schedules MSG3 transmission

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `13415731`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
SCell 5G-L2-PS sends UlData\_PuschReceiveReq to 5G-L1 with grant same as MSG3 transmission slot included in PsPeerCtrl\_ScellRequestRarTransmissionInd.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-12**  (ID: `13415732`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(12) PCell 5G-L2-PS sends Random Access Request

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-12.0-1**  (ID: `13415733`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
PCell 5G-L2-PS selects slot for Random Acces Request transmission so that UE will transmit its first uplink transmission on SCell (MSG3) in slot requested by SCell.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-13**  (ID: `13415736`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(13) 5G-L1 transmits Random Access Response

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-13.0-1**  (ID: `13415737`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
5G-L1 on Pcell side sends PDSCH with Random Access Response to UE.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-14**  (ID: `13415738`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(14) UE sends MSG3

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-14.0-1**  (ID: `13415739`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
Ue preforms first uplink transmission on SCell side in slot assigned by SCell 5G-L2-PS in PsPeerCtrl\_ScellRequestRarTransmissionInd.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-15**  (ID: `13415740`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(15) 5G-L1 notifies 5G-L2-PS about MSG3 transmission

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-15.0-1**  (ID: `13415741`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
5G-L1 sends UlData\_PuschReceiveReq to 5G-L2-PS. This concludes Timing Alignment procedure. At this point SCell 5G-L2-PS has confirmation UE uses correct Timing Advance values for uplink transmission.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-16**  (ID: `13417534`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(16) SCell 5G-L2-PS stops timer

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-16.0-1**  (ID: `13417535`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
As procedure reached success condition timer shall be stopped as early as possible.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-17**  (ID: `13415744`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(17) SCell 5G-L2-PS releases preamble

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-17.0-1**  (ID: `13415745`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
5G-L2-PS sends PsUser\_ReleaseCfraPreambleInd (message definition: [13381586: PsUser\_ReleaseCfraPreambleInd](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX__nQf5gAhEfGhFrIQm2O4Ew)) to 5G-CP-RT releasing preamble reserved for PDCCH Order procedure.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-18**  (ID: `13415748`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(18) SCell 5G-L2-PS notifies PCell 5G-L2-PS about successful Timing Alignment procedure.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-18.0-1**  (ID: `13415749`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
SCell 5G-L2-PS responds with PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq to PCell (message definition: [10979530: PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingResp message content:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_Eov7YPu5Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). At this point PCell is informed about UE having Timing Advance in SCell aligned and now uplink transmission can be started.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-19**  (ID: `13415750`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(19) SCell 5G-L2-PS notifies PCell 5G-L2-PS about unsuccessful Timing Alignment procedure.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-19.0-1**  (ID: `13415751`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
SCell 5G-L2-PS responds with PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq to PCell with status EStatus5G\_NotOk. Procedure is failed for UE and can be restarted after backoff time.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-20**  (ID: `13415752`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(20) SCell 5G-L2-PS stops timer

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-20.0-1**  (ID: `13415753`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
As procedure failed timer shall be stopped.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-21**  (ID: `13417562`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(21) Procedure timeout timer expired

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-21.0-1**  (ID: `13417563`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
Procedure could not be finished within maximum number of preamble transmission attempts.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-22**  (ID: `13417564`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(22) SCell 5G-L2-PS releases preamble

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-22.0-1**  (ID: `13417565`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
5G-L2-PS sends PsUser\_ReleaseCfraPreambleInd to 5G-CP-RT releasing preamble reserved for PDCCH Order procedure.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-23**  (ID: `13417566`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(23) SCell 5G-L2-PS notifies PCell 5G-L2-PS about unsuccessful Timing Alignment procedure.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-23.0-1**  (ID: `13417567`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
SCell 5G-L2-PS responds with PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingResp to PCell with status EStatus5G\_NotOk. Procedure is failed for UE and can be restarted after backoff time.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-24**  (ID: `13492546`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(24) PCell 5G-L2-PS requests SCell 5G-L2-PS to abort Timing Alignment procedure.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-24.0-1**  (ID: `13492547`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
When Beam Failure Recovery is detected PCell 5G-L2-PS sends PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq with modifcation type abort UL timing alignement procedure.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-25**  (ID: `13492582`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(25) SCell 5G-L2-PS stops timer

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-25.0-1**  (ID: `13492583`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
As procedure is aborted timer shall be stopped.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-26**  (ID: `13492584`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(26) SCell 5G-L2-PS releases preamble

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-26.0-1**  (ID: `13492585`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
As procedure is aborted and UE will not use preamble for PDCCH Order procedure, 5G-L2-PS sends PsUser\_ReleaseCfraPreambleInd to 5G-CP-RT releasing it.

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-27**  (ID: `13492587`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
(27) SCell confirms successful abort of Timing Alignement Porcedure

---

**6.1.30.0-2.0-27.0-1**  (ID: `13492588`)

Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG
SCell 5G-L2-PS responds with PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq to PCell with status EStatus5G\_NotOk for abort request. Procedure is aborted for UE and can be restarted after backoff time. No other communication related to procedure on SCell side is expected.

---

### 6.1.30.0-3 Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG Exception (ID: 13415687)
